04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 268: float G_GGX_Smith( const in float alpha, const in float dotNL, const in float dotNV ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 269: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 270: 	float gl = dotNL + sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNL ) );

04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 272: 	return 1.0 / ( gl * gv );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 273: }
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 274: float G_GGX_SmithCorrelated( const in float alpha, const in float dotNL, const in float dotNV ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 275: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 276: 	float gv = dotNL * sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNV ) );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 277: 	float gl = dotNV * sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNL ) );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 278: 	return 0.5 / max( gv + gl, EPSILON );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 279: }
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 280: float D_GGX( const in float alpha, const in float dotNH ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 281: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );

04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 283: 	return RECIPROCAL_PI * a2 / pow2( denom );

04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 748: 	vec2 cubeToUV( vec3 v, float texelSizeY ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 749: 		vec3 absV = abs( v );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 750: 		float scaleToCube = 1.0 / max( absV.x, max( absV.y, absV.z ) );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 751: 		absV *= scaleToCube;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 752: 		v *= scaleToCube * ( 1.0 - 2.0 * texelSizeY );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 753: 		vec2 planar = v.xy;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 754: 		float almostATexel = 1.5 * texelSizeY;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 755: 		float almostOne = 1.0 - almostATexel;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 756: 		if ( absV.z >= almostOne ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 757: 			if ( v.z > 0.0 )
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 758: 				planar.x = 4.0 - v.x;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 759: 		} else if ( absV.x >= almostOne ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 760: 			float signX = sign( v.x );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 761: 			planar.x = v.z * signX + 2.0 * signX;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 762: 		} else if ( absV.y >= almostOne ) {
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 763: 			float signY = sign( v.y );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 764: 			planar.x = v.x + 2.0 * signY + 2.0;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 765: 			planar.y = v.z * signY - 2.0;
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 766: 		}
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 767: 		return vec2( 0.125, 0.25 ) * planar + vec2( 0.375, 0.75 );
04-11 17:44:16.548  8872  8893 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 768: 	}

04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 268: float G_GGX_Smith( const in float alpha, const in float dotNL, const in float dotNV ) {
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 269: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 270: 	float gl = dotNL + sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNL ) );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 271: 	float gv = dotNV + sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNV ) );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 272: 	return 1.0 / ( gl * gv );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 273: }
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 274: float G_GGX_SmithCorrelated( const in float alpha, const in float dotNL, const in float dotNV ) {
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 275: 	float a2 = pow2( alpha );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 276: 	float gv = dotNL * sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNV ) );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 277: 	float gl = dotNV * sqrt( a2 + ( 1.0 - a2 ) * pow2( dotNL ) );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 278: 	return 0.5 / max( gv + gl, EPSILON );
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 279: }
04-11 17:45:27.910  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 280: float D_GGX( const in float alpha, const in float dotNH ) {

04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 748: 	vec2 cubeToUV( vec3 v, float texelSizeY ) {
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 749: 		vec3 absV = abs( v );
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 750: 		float scaleToCube = 1.0 / max( absV.x, max( absV.y, absV.z ) );
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 751: 		absV *= scaleToCube;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 752: 		v *= scaleToCube * ( 1.0 - 2.0 * texelSizeY );
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 753: 		vec2 planar = v.xy;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 754: 		float almostATexel = 1.5 * texelSizeY;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 755: 		float almostOne = 1.0 - almostATexel;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 756: 		if ( absV.z >= almostOne ) {
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 757: 			if ( v.z > 0.0 )
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 758: 				planar.x = 4.0 - v.x;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 759: 		} else if ( absV.x >= almostOne ) {
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 760: 			float signX = sign( v.x );
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 761: 			planar.x = v.z * signX + 2.0 * signX;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 762: 		} else if ( absV.y >= almostOne ) {
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 763: 			float signY = sign( v.y );
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 764: 			planar.x = v.x + 2.0 * signY + 2.0;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 765: 			planar.y = v.z * signY - 2.0;
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 766: 		}
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 767: 		return vec2( 0.125, 0.25 ) * planar + vec2( 0.375, 0.75 );
04-11 17:45:27.911  9012  9032 D RustAndroidGlueStdouterr: 768: 	}
